#### Exercise 8.21(a)
* **Mathematical Target:** construct `Œªa.a¬ß`, show it is computable, and prove `a‚â§I ‚üπ a¬ß‚â§I` (half of "`a` a projection ‚üπ `a¬ß` a projection")
* **Lean File:** `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise821.lean`
* **Proof Notes:** The construction of `a¬ß` and its tractable properties. **`U¬ß ‚ä¥ U`** (`dsharpU_trianglelefteq_U`): `dsharpPresentation` (Prop 7.7) makes `U¬ß` effectively given, so `theorem_8_8_b_strong` hands it a computable projection pair `iSharp : U¬ß‚ÜíU`/`jSharp : U‚ÜíU¬ß`, exactly Definition 8.9's own `i‚Çä/j‚Çä` etc. recipe. **The operator** (`aSharp`): Scott's `a¬ß` should satisfy `a¬ß(x¬ß)=(a x)¬ß` and `a¬ß‚ü®y,z‚ü©=‚ü®a¬ß y,a¬ß z‚ü©` ‚Äî precisely the two defining equations (`gMap_in`/`gMap_pair`) of Exercise 7.17 Part 2's catamorphism `gMap` specialized to `u:=in‚àòa`, `v:=pair`, so the "fixed-point construction" the exercise asks for is already on hand as `gMap`: `aSharpInner a := gMap (inSharpMap.comp a) pairSharpMap hU : U¬ß‚ÜíU¬ß`, `aSharp a := iSharp‚àòaSharpInner a‚àòjSharp : U‚ÜíU`, mirroring Definition 8.9's conjugation-through-a-projection-pair pattern. **Computable** (`aSharp_isComputable`): `gMap_isComputable` applies directly since `in`/`pair` are computable, chained through `iSharp`/`jSharp`'s own computability. **`a‚â§I ‚üπ a¬ß‚â§I`** (`aSharp_le_idMap_of_le`, half of "`a` a projection ‚üπ `a¬ß` a projection", Prop 8.10's `a‚äëI ‚üπ a+b‚äëI+I=i‚àòj‚äëI` recipe transcribed to `¬ß`): needs two new general tools ‚Äî **`gMap_mono`** (monotonicity of the catamorphism in `u,v`, by direct structural induction on the `GRel` derivation parallel to `gRel_mono`, using `ApproximableMap.le_iff`'s unfolding of `‚â§` to pointwise relation inclusion) and **`gMap_inSharp_pairSharp_eq_idMap`** (`gMap in pair = I_{D¬ß}`, by two structural inductions ‚Äî on `GRel` and on `MemS` ‚Äî mirroring `gMap_in`/`gMap_pair`'s own style). `lake build` (whole project) green, zero `sorry`. Axiom audit: `dsharpU_trianglelefteq_U`/`aSharp_isComputable`/`aSharp_le_idMap_of_le ‚äÜ {propext, Classical.choice, Quot.sound}` (inherited from `U`, not new, matching `Definition89.lean`/`Proposition810.lean`'s baseline); the two new general tools `gMap_mono`/`gMap_inSharp_pairSharp_eq_idMap` are fully choice-free `‚äÜ {propext, Quot.sound}`.

#### Exercise 8.21(b)
* **Mathematical Target:** the other half of "`a` a projection ‚üπ `a¬ß` a projection" ‚Äî idempotence `a=a‚àòa ‚üπ a¬ß=a¬ß‚àòa¬ß`, completing `isProjection_aSharp` (Proposition 8.10's recipe, transcribed to `¬ß`, for the retraction half rather than the `‚â§I` half already done in 8.21(a))
* **Lean File:** `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise821.lean`
* **Proof Notes:** Unlike `√ó`/`‚Üí`/`+` in `Proposition810.lean`, there is no elementwise closed form for `gMap`'s action on a *general* element of `D¬ß` (its elements can be infinite trees, unlike `pair`/`fst`/`snd` or `curry`/`eval`, which have one-step defining equations valid everywhere), so this needs a genuine catamorphism-uniqueness lemma. All four planned sub-steps closed: **8.21(b)(1) ‚Äî `gMap_eq_of_satisfies`** (the uniqueness-of-catamorphism lemma: any *strict* `k : Dsharp D hD ‚Üí E` satisfying `gMap`'s two defining equations at the element level equals `gMap u v hD` outright). Rather than the anticipated heavyweight order-theoretic bound (√Ý la `Theorem614.lean`'s initial-algebra uniqueness), a direct induction on the `MemS`-derivation of the input neighbourhood suffices: `k`'s abstract relation is pinned at each `MemS`-shape by evaluating the assumed element-level hypothesis at the shape's own **principal element**, via `rel_iff_mem_principal` plus two new "principal of the constructor is the constructor of principals" bridge identities (`inSharp_principal : inSharp D hD (D.principal hX) = (Dsharp D hD).principal (MemS.zero hX)`, proved by chaining `inSharpMap_rel`/`inSharpMap_toElementMap`/`rel_iff_mem_principal`; `pairSharp_principal`, analogously via `pairSharpMap_rel`/`pairSharpMap_toElementMap` and a new general product-level identity `pair_principal_eq_principal_prodNbhd : pair (V‚ÇÄ.principal hP) (V‚ÇÅ.principal hQ) = (prod V‚ÇÄ V‚ÇÅ).principal (prod_mem_prodNbhd hP hQ)`). **8.21(b)(2) ‚Äî `gMap_selfComp_eq_of_isRetraction`** (general form, for any `D`/`hD`/retraction `a : D‚ÜíD`): `(gMap u v hD).comp (gMap u v hD) = gMap u v hD` where `u := (inSharpMap hD).comp a`, `v := pairSharpMap hD` ‚Äî applying **(b)(1)** to `k := g.comp g`, whose two defining equations reduce (via `gMap_in`/`gMap_pair` applied twice, chained through `a`'s own idempotence) to the equations for `g` itself; `aSharpInner_idem_of_isRetraction` specializes this at `D:=U` (`aSharpInner_eq` unfolds `aSharpInner` to the literal `gMap` expression, `rfl`). **8.21(b)(3) ‚Äî `isRetraction_aSharp`.** Transports idempotence of `aSharpInner a` through the projection pair `iSharp`/`jSharp` to `(aSharp a).comp (aSharp a) = aSharp a`, via `toElementMap_aSharp` (the one-step unfolding, mirroring `toElementMap_prodComb`/`toElementMap_arrowComb`) plus the exact `toElementMap_of_comp_eq_idMap`/`toElementMap_idem_of_isRetraction` recipe `Proposition810.lean`'s `isRetraction_prodComb`/`isRetraction_arrowComb` already use, conjugated through `jSharp_comp_iSharp` instead of `jTimes_comp_iTimes`/`jArrow_comp_iArrow`. **8.21(b)(4) ‚Äî `isProjection_aSharp`.** Packages **8.21(a)**'s `aSharp_le_idMap_of_le` with **(b)(3)**'s `isRetraction_aSharp` into `IsProjection a ‚Üí IsProjection (aSharp a)`, completing "`a` projection ‚üπ `a¬ß` projection" in full, matching `Proposition810.lean`'s `isProjection_sumComb`/`isProjection_prodComb`/`isProjection_arrowComb`. `lake build` green, zero `sorry`. Axiom audit: `gMap_eq_of_satisfies`/`gMap_selfComp_eq_of_isRetraction`/`aSharpInner_idem_of_isRetraction`/`isRetraction_aSharp`/`isProjection_aSharp ‚äÜ {propext, Classical.choice, Quot.sound}` (inherited from `U`, matching 8.21(a)'s own baseline, nothing new); the three bridge identities (`inSharp_principal`/`pairSharp_principal`/`pair_principal_eq_principal_prodNbhd`) are fully choice-free `‚äÜ {propext, Quot.sound}`.

#### Exercise 8.21(c)
* **Mathematical Target:** the headline isomorphism `D_{a¬ß} ‚âÖ (D_a)¬ß` for `a` a finitary projection of `U`
* **Lean File:** `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise821.lean`
* **Proof Notes:** The originally-planned route (via `fixedNbhd`-level transport plus a Theorem-6.14-style initial-algebra uniqueness argument on the sub-tree-algebra cut out by `a`'s fixed points) turned out to be avoidable entirely, by noticing `D ‚Ü¶ D¬ß` is *functorial on morphisms*, not just on domains ‚Äî reducing 8.21(c) to a direct instance of `Proposition810b.lean`'s own `elementIsoOfProjectionPair` recipe (exactly as used there for `D_{a+b}‚âÖD_a+D_b` etc.), with no new order-theoretic machinery needed. **`dsharpMap`** (the functor's action on morphisms): precomposing `inSharpMap` with any `f : D‚ÇÅ ‚Üí D‚ÇÄ` and recursing via `gMap` extends `f` to `dsharpMap f : D‚ÇÅ¬ß ‚Üí D‚ÇÄ¬ß := gMap ((inSharpMap hD‚ÇÄ).comp f) (pairSharpMap hD‚ÇÄ) hD‚ÇÅ`; `aSharpInner a` is the special case `D‚ÇÄ=D‚ÇÅ=U`, `f:=a` (`dsharpMap_self_eq_aSharpInner`, `rfl`). **Functor laws**: `dsharpMap_id` (`id¬ß=id`) is literally `gMap_inSharp_pairSharp_eq_idMap` after `comp_idMap`; `dsharpMap_comp` (`(f'‚àòf)¬ß=f'¬ß‚àòf¬ß`, for *any* `f,f'`, no retraction hypothesis) applies `gMap_eq_of_satisfies` to `k:=(dsharpMap f').comp(dsharpMap f)` ‚Äî verbatim 8.21(b)'s `gMap_selfComp_eq_of_isRetraction` proof strategy, but simpler since composing two *different* maps needs no idempotence step. **The projection pair** (`ISharpComb`/`JSharpComb`): transporting `iSharp`/`jSharp` through `dsharpMap`'s action on `(fixedNbhd_subsystem a).inj/.proj` (the canonical injection/projection pair of `D_a := fixedNbhd a ‚óÅ U`, Proposition 6.12) gives `I:(D_a)¬ß‚ÜíU`, `J:U‚Üí(D_a)¬ß` with **`J‚àòI = I_{(D_a)¬ß}`** (`JSharpComb_comp_ISharpComb`, unconditional: the functor laws turn `j_a‚àòi_a=I_{D_a}` (`Subsystem.proj_comp_inj`) directly into `J‚àòI=I_{(D_a)¬ß}`) and, when `a` is a finitary projection, **`I‚àòJ = a¬ß`** (`ISharpComb_comp_JSharpComb`: the functor laws turn `i_a‚àòj_a=a` (Theorem 8.6's `inj_comp_proj_eq_self`) into `dsharpMap` applied to `a`, i.e. `aSharpInner a` via `dsharpMap_self_eq_aSharpInner`, giving exactly `aSharp`'s own defining equation `aSharp_eq`). **Assembly** (`dsharp_fixedNbhd_elementIso`): `elementIsoOfProjectionPair I J (J‚àòI=id) (a¬ß=I‚àòJ)` hands us `(D_a)¬ß.Element ‚âÉo Fix(a¬ß)` directly ‚Äî Scott's `D_{a¬ß}‚âÖ(D_a)¬ß`, in the same "domain of a projection = its `toElementMap`-fixed-point set" convention `Proposition810b.lean` already uses. This simultaneously reproves `IsFinitary (a¬ß)` (`isFinitary_aSharp`, via `isFinitary_of_projectionPair`), so combined with 8.21(a)/(b)'s `isProjection_aSharp`, **`isFinitaryProjection_aSharp`**: `a` a finitary projection of `U` `‚üπ` `a¬ß` a finitary projection, completing Exercise 8.21 in full. `lake build` (whole project) green, zero `sorry`. Axiom audit: `dsharpMap`/`dsharpMap_id` (mentioning no `U`) are choice-free `‚äÜ {propext, Quot.sound}`; `dsharpMap_comp`/`JSharpComb_comp_ISharpComb`/`ISharpComb_comp_JSharpComb`/`dsharp_fixedNbhd_elementIso`/`isFinitary_aSharp`/`isFinitaryProjection_aSharp` `‚äÜ {propext, Classical.choice, Quot.sound}` (inherited from `U`/`gMap_eq_of_satisfies`, matching 8.21(a)/(b)'s own baseline, nothing new).

#### Exercise 8.22
* **Mathematical Target:** which of `B ‚ä¥ C`/`C ‚ä¥ B` holds for Example 6.2's `B ‚âÖ B+B`, `C ‚âÖ ùüô+C+C`; the general `D=T(D)+S(D)`, `E=T(E)` case; the projections visible in 6.2
* **Lean File:** `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise822.lean`
* **Proof Notes:** **Both directions hold.** `B ‚ä¥ C` (`B_trianglelefteq_C`): `B`/`C` share tokens `Str` with `B.mem ‚äÜ C.mem` (every `B`-cone is already a `C`-neighbourhood), so `B` is a *literal* subsystem `B ‚óÅ C` (Definition 6.10) ‚Äî `inter_closed` follows from `cone_trichotomy` plus `C_nonempty` ruling out the disjoint case ‚Äî and `Lemma615.Subsystem.trianglelefteq` hands us `B ‚ä¥ C` directly; the projection pair is the identity inclusion `i:B‚ÜíC` and the "collapse completions back onto their cone" retraction `j:C‚ÜíB`, exactly Scott's hinted projection. `C ‚ä¥ B` (`C_trianglelefteq_B`) is the substantive direction, since `C`'s completed-sequence elements `‚Üë{œÉ}` have no counterpart in `B`: built via a concrete bit-doubling re-encoding of tokens, `enc œÉ` (`enc[]=[]`, `enc(b::œÉ)=b::b::enc œÉ`) for `C`'s cones and `encC œÉ := enc œÉ ++ [true,false]` (a two-bit marker `[b,b]` can never produce) for `C`'s singletons. A suite of structural-induction lemmas (`enc_prefix_iff`, `enc_injective`, `enc_prefix_encC_iff`, `not_encC_prefix_enc`, `encC_prefix_encC_iff`, `encC_injective`) shows this re-encoding exactly reproduces `C`'s own cone/singleton nesting-or-disjointness pattern inside `B`. The image family `D' := {cone(enc œÉ)} ‚à™ {cone(encC œÉ)}` is a `NeighborhoodSystem` (`NeighborhoodSystem.ofNestedOrDisjoint`, using `D'_nestedOrDisjoint` from `cone_trichotomy` on the encoded cones) and a literal subsystem `D' ‚óÅ B` (`D'_subsystem_B`). The order-isomorphism `cdEquiv : C.Element ‚âÉo D'.Element` is built from mutually-inverse filter maps `toD'`/`fromD'` (mirroring `Example62.toBB`/`fromBB`), with membership-characterization lemmas (`toD'_mem_enc`, `toD'_mem_encC`, `fromD'_mem_cone`, `fromD'_mem_singleton`) driving both the `left_inv`/`right_inv` proofs and `map_rel_iff'`; `C ‚âÖ·¥∞ D'` plus `D' ‚óÅ B` gives `C ‚ä¥ B` via `Lemma615.Trianglelefteq`'s definition directly. **General case** (`D=T(D)+S(D)`, `E=T(E)` ‚üπ `E ‚ä¥ D`): argued in prose in the module docstring rather than re-derived in Lean ‚Äî instantiating `T(X):=X+X`, `S(X):=ùüô` recovers exactly `B`(`=E`)/`C`(`=D`) above; the general pattern is that `D‚âÖT(D)+S(D)` always gives a *projection pair* `T(D)‚ä¥D` (not merely an embedding), and running `Theorem616.lean`'s approximant-chain argument with this projection pair standing in for the Lambek isomorphism (one side weakened from iso to retraction) produces a genuine projection pair `E‚áÑD` from `E`'s own `T(E)‚âÖE` and initiality ‚Äî a full re-derivation would duplicate `Theorem616.lean`'s ~250 lines with one hypothesis weakened, so only the concrete `B`/`C` instance is formally checked. `lake build` green, zero `sorry`. Axiom audit: `B_trianglelefteq_C`/`C_trianglelefteq_B ‚äÜ {propext, Quot.sound}` (fully choice-free).

#### Exercise 8.23
* **Mathematical Target:** if `t:(U‚ÜíU)‚Üí(U‚ÜíU)` is computable, sends finitary projections `a` to finitary projections `t(a)` with `D_{t(a)} ‚âÖ T(D_a)`, does `‚Äñt‚Äñ=fix(t)` solve `D_{‚Äñt‚Äñ}‚âÖT(D_{‚Äñt‚Äñ})` initially w.r.t. projections, effectively?
* **Lean File:** `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise823.lean`
* **Proof Notes:** **Yes to all three, two formalized in full, one in prose.** `t` is modelled as an approximable self-map of the function space `t : ApproximableMap (funSpace E E) (funSpace E E)` (general `E`, not just `U`), with `tOp t a := toApproxMap (t.toElementMap (toFilter a))` the induced operator on actual maps and `fixOp t := toApproxMap t.fixElement` (Theorem 4.1) Scott's `‚Äñt‚Äñ`. **Claim 1** (`isFinitaryProjection_fixOp`): given `ht : ‚àÄa, IsFinitaryProjection a ‚Üí IsFinitaryProjection (tOp t a)`, `‚Äñt‚Äñ` is itself a finitary projection ‚Äî proved via **Theorem 8.6's `sub` combinator** rather than re-deriving Theorem 6.16's colimit-of-domains machinery: by induction every approximant `t.iterElem n` is (under `toApproxMap`) a finitary projection (base case `n=0` is the constant-bottom map `constMap E E.bot`, shown finitary directly ‚Äî idempotent/`‚â§I` by bare unfolding, finitary because `Fix(‚ä•)={‚ä•}` is order-iso to the terminal system `unitSys`; step case is `ht`), hence a fixed point of `sub`/`subFilter`; `subFilter` already commutes with directed unions (`Theorem86.lean`'s `Sub8_6.subFilter_iSupDirected`, since `sub`'s formula is a positive existential), so it fixes `t.fixElement = ‚äî‚Çô t.iterElem n` too, giving `sub ‚Äñt‚Äñ = ‚Äñt‚Äñ` i.e. `IsFinitaryProjection ‚Äñt‚Äñ`. **Claim 2, the equation** (`fixedDomain_fixOp_iso_T`): `‚Äñt‚Äñ` is a *genuine* (not merely approximate) fixed point, `tOp t (fixOp t) = fixOp t` (`tOp_fixOp`, from `toElementMap_fixElement`); substituting `a:=‚Äñt‚Äñ` into an abstractly-packaged hypothesis `hT a : Fix(t(a)) ‚âÖ T(a)` and rewriting `t(‚Äñt‚Äñ)=‚Äñt‚Äñ` gives `Fix(‚Äñt‚Äñ) ‚âÖ T(‚Äñt‚Äñ)` *unconditionally* ‚Äî a one-line substitution, not a colimit argument, precisely because `‚Äñt‚Äñ` solves the equation exactly. **Claim 2, initiality** (`fixedNbhd_fixOp_subsystem`): for any other finitary projection `a` with `tOp t a ‚â§ a` (covering every alternative exact solution), Theorem 4.1's minimality (`fixElement_le_of_toElementMap_le`) gives `‚Äñt‚Äñ ‚â§ a`, and Exercise 8.16's order-isomorphism `a‚â§b ‚Üî D_a‚óÅD_b` upgrades this to `D_{‚Äñt‚Äñ} ‚óÅ D_a` (hence `‚ä¥`, Lemma 6.15) ‚Äî literally "the initial solution with respect to projections". **Claim 3, effectiveness**: left in prose (module docstring), matching this codebase's own precedent of deferring Theorem 8.6's computability clause (needs Definition 7.1's `ComputablePresentation` machinery threaded through a directed union of presentations ‚Äî the same style of argument Theorem 8.8(b)/(c) already carry out for their own effective limiting construction, not repeated here). `lake build` (whole project, 3188 jobs) green, zero `sorry`. Axiom audit: `isFinitaryProjection_fixOp`/`tOp_fixOp`/`fixedDomain_fixOp_iso_T`/`fixedNbhd_fixOp_subsystem` all `‚äÜ {propext, Quot.sound}` (fully choice-free).

#### Exercise 8.24
* **Mathematical Target:** binary constructs `S,T` ‚üπ a pair of effectively presented domains
* **Lean File:** `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise824.lean`
* **Proof Notes:** **The two-variable generalization of Exercise 8.23, reduced to a single instance of Exercise 8.23's own machinery run on the product function space.** Scott's `s,t : (E‚ÜíE)√ó(E‚ÜíE) ‚Üí (E‚ÜíE)` are modelled as approximable maps `s t : ApproximableMap PairSpace (funSpace E E)` out of the pair space `PairSpace := prod (funSpace E E) (funSpace E E)`, with `binOp s a b := toApproxMap (s.toElementMap (pair (toFilter a)(toFilter b)))` Scott's `s(a,b)` (and likewise `binOp t a b`). The two combine into **one** self-map of the pair space, `paired s t : ApproximableMap PairSpace PairSpace` (Definition 3.3's pairing), to which Theorem 4.1 applies exactly as in 8.23; its exact fixed point splits via `.fst`/`.snd` (Definition 3.1's projections) into `aStar s t`/`bStar s t` ‚Äî Scott's simultaneous solution `(‚Äñs‚Äñ,‚Äñt‚Äñ)`. **Claim 1** (`isFinitaryProjection_aStar_bStar`): given `hst : ‚àÄa b, IsFinitaryProjection a ‚Üí IsFinitaryProjection b ‚Üí IsFinitaryProjection (binOp s a b) ‚àß IsFinitaryProjection (binOp t a b)`, both `aStar s t`/`bStar s t` are finitary projections ‚Äî induction (`isFinitaryProjection_chain`) shows every approximant pair `(aOp s t n, bOp s t n)` (`.fst`/`.snd` of `(paired s t).iterElem n`, satisfying the mutual recursion `aOp_succ`/`bOp_succ`, base case the constant-bottom map reusing 8.23's `isFinitaryProjection_constMap_bot`) consists of finitary projections; the genuinely new step is transporting Theorem 8.6's `subFilter`-commutes-with-directed-sups argument through `.fst`/`.snd`: `(paired s t).fixElement.fst` is identified with `‚äî‚Çô(aOp s t n)`'s filter via a direct membership chase (`hEqA`, through `mem_fst`/`mem_fixElement`/`mem_iterElem`), and `subFilter` fixes it termwise hence fixes the union (`hkeyA`, `Sub8_6.subFilter_iSupDirected`) ‚Äî 8.23's Claim 1 argument, run twice. **Claim 2** (`fixedDomain_aStar_bStar_iso`): `(aStar s t, bStar s t)` is a *genuine* simultaneous fixed point (`binOp_aStar_bStar_left/right`, from `toElementMap_fixElement`+`toElementMap_paired`+`fst_pair`/`snd_pair`/`pair_fst_snd`, bare substitution not a colimit argument); substituting into abstractly-packaged `hS a b : Fix(binOp s a b) ‚âÖ S(a,b)`/`hT a b : Fix(binOp t a b) ‚âÖ T(a,b)` gives `Fix(aStar s t) ‚âÖ S(aStar s t,bStar s t)`, `Fix(bStar s t) ‚âÖ T(aStar s t,bStar s t)` unconditionally ‚Äî Scott's `D‚âÖS(D,E)`, `E‚âÖT(D,E)`. **Initiality** (`fixedNbhd_aStar_bStar_subsystem`): any other pre-fixed-point pair `(a,b)` (`binOp s a b ‚â§ a`, `binOp t a b ‚â§ b`) packaged as `pair(toFilter a)(toFilter b)` gives, via `pair_le_pair_iff` + Theorem 4.1's minimality + Exercise 8.16's `a‚â§b ‚Üî D_a‚óÅD_b`, both `fixedNbhd(aStar s t)‚óÅfixedNbhd a` and `fixedNbhd(bStar s t)‚óÅfixedNbhd b` simultaneously. **Effectiveness**: prose only (module docstring), matching 8.23's own deferred computability clause, doubled (joint induction that computable `s,t` make every approximant pair computable, then the simultaneous limit computable by the effective-limit-of-effective-chain argument already used for Theorem 8.8's `Y‚Çô`-chain). `lake build` (whole project, 3189 jobs) green, zero `sorry`. Axiom audit: `isFinitaryProjection_aStar_bStar`/`fixedDomain_aStar_bStar_iso`/`fixedNbhd_aStar_bStar_subsystem` all `‚äÜ {propext, Quot.sound}` (fully choice-free).

#### Exercise 8.25
* **Mathematical Target:** a non-trivial domain `D` (`D ‚âá ùüô`) with `D ‚âÖ D ‚Üí D`; is `D` effectively given?
* **Lean File:** `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise825.lean` (+ `Exercise825Unit.lean`, `Exercise825Pow.lean`, `Exercise825Embed.lean`, `Exercise825Congr.lean`, `Exercise825Closing.lean`, `Exercise825FixedPoint.lean`)
* **Proof Notes:** **Follows Scott's own hint chain exactly, six steps.** **(1) the "obvious" solution is trivial** (`Exercise825Unit.lean`): `funSpace_unitSys_isomorphic : (ùüô‚Üíùüô) ‚âÖ ùüô` (`Unique`-to-`Unique` `OrderIso`, since both `ùüô`'s element poset and `ApproximableMap ùüô ùüô`'s are singletons) ‚Äî solving `D‚âÖD‚ÜíV` from `V=ùüô` is stuck forever at `ùüô`, motivating the switch to `V:=ùí∞^‚àû`. **(2) `ùí∞^‚àû√óùí∞^‚àû‚âÖùí∞^‚àû`** (`Exercise825Pow.lean`, `pow_prod_isomorphic`, `V:=iterSys U`): built from `powProdOrderIso`, chaining `prodEquiv`/`iterSeqEquiv` (Exercise 3.16's `D^‚àû‚âÉo(‚Ñï‚Üí|D|)`) through a genuine `(‚Ñï‚ÜíE)√ó(‚Ñï‚ÜíE)‚âÉo(‚Ñï‚ÜíE)` "interleaving" order-isomorphism (`interleaveOrderIso`, built from a new general `sumArrowOrderIso : ((Œ±‚äïŒ≤)‚ÜíE)‚âÉo(Œ±‚ÜíE)√ó(Œ≤‚ÜíE)` and `piCongrOrderIso` reindexed along `Mathlib`'s `Equiv.natSumNatEquivNat:‚Ñï‚äï‚Ñï‚âÉ‚Ñï`). **(3) `D‚âÖD‚Üíùí∞^‚àû` by the fixed-point method** (`Exercise825FixedPoint.lean`, the technical core): `ùí∞^‚àû` effectively given (Exercise 7.15's `iterSys_isEffectivelyGiven`) `‚üπ` Theorem 8.8(b)'s `theorem_8_8_b_strong` gives a projection pair `ùí∞^‚àû‚áÑùí∞`; `c:=i‚àòj` is then a finitary projection with `Fix(c)‚âÖùí∞^‚àû` (`fixedNbhd_cCombinator_isomorphic`, via Proposition 8.10(b)'s generic `elementIsoOfProjectionPair`/Theorem 8.6's `inj_comp_proj_eq_self` bridge). The genuinely new construction is making `t(a):=a‚Üíc` (Definition 8.9's `arrowComb(-) c`) **continuous in `a`**, not just a family indexed by `a`: a joint three-variable evaluator `R(œà,œÜ,x):=c(œÜ(œà(x)))` built purely from `evalMap`/`proj`/`paired` (`RMap`, manifestly jointly continuous), curried *twice* via Table 5.5's `curry`/`curryC` (`lamOp`) to recover `expMap(-) c = lamComb(-) c` at every fixed `a` (`toApproxMap_lamOp`, checked against `Proposition810b.toApproxMap_toElementMap_expMap` by unwinding both curry layers), then conjugated by the *fixed* projection pair `ùí∞‚áÑ(ùí∞‚Üíùí∞)` via `expMap jArrow iArrow` to land exactly on `arrowComb a c` (`tOpMap`/`tOp_tOpMap`). `ht_tOpMap` (Proposition 8.10(b)'s `finitaryProjection_arrowComb`) plus Exercise 8.23's abstract machinery (`isFinitaryProjection_fixOp`, `fixedDomain_fixOp_iso_T` instantiated at `T(a):=funSpace(fixedNbhd a)(fixedNbhd c)`, via `arrowComb_elementIso`) hand us `D‚âÖD‚Üíùí∞^‚àû` for `D:=fixedNbhd(fixOp(tOpMap c))` (`Dsol_isomorphic_funSpace_cCombinator`). **(4) `ùí∞‚ä¥D`, non-trivial/universal** (`U_trianglelefteq_Dsol`): chains `ùí∞‚ä¥ùí∞^‚àû` (`Exercise825Embed.lean`'s `trianglelefteq_iterSys`, the "singleton stack" embedding `x‚Ü¶‚ü®x,‚ä•,‚ä•,‚Ä¶‚ü©` with `head` as retraction, reusing Exercise 5.11's stack combinators and Exercise 6.18's `component_bot`), `ùí∞^‚àû‚âÖfixedNbhd c`, the *general* constant-function embedding `V‚ä¥(D‚ÜíV)` (`Exercise820.lean`'s `trianglelefteq_funSpace_const`, already on hand ‚Äî `b‚Ü¶(Œª_.b)`/evaluation-at-`‚ä•`), and `D‚Üíùí∞^‚àû‚âÖD` reversed. **(5)/(6) `D√óD‚âÖD` and `D‚âÖD‚ÜíD`** (`Exercise825Closing.lean`, a fully abstract closing argument taking `hDV:D‚âÖD‚ÜíV`, `hVV:V√óV‚âÖV` for arbitrary `D,V`): `prod_self_isomorphic` chains `D√óD‚âÖ(D‚ÜíV)√ó(D‚ÜíV)‚âÖD‚Üí(V√óV)‚âÖD‚ÜíV‚âÖD` (using a new `funSpace_congr`/`curry_isomorphic` toolkit, `Exercise825Congr.lean` ‚Äî built via a standalone `orderIsoOfMutualInverse` gadget upgrading *exact* mutual-inverse `ApproximableMap`s to an `OrderIso`, applied to `Proposition810b.expMap`'s functor laws); `funSpace_self_isomorphic` then chains `D‚ÜíD‚âÖD‚Üí(D‚ÜíV)‚âÖ(D√óD)‚ÜíV‚âÖD‚ÜíV‚âÖD`, reusing `prod_self_isomorphic`. Instantiating at `V:=fixedNbhd c` (with `hVV_cCombinator` transported from step (2) along `fixedNbhd c‚âÖùí∞^‚àû`) gives `exercise_8_25_main`. **Effectiveness**: prose only (module docstring of `Exercise825.lean`), matching Theorem 8.6/Exercise 8.23's own deferred computability clauses for the identical reason (needs Definition 7.1's `ComputablePresentation` machinery threaded through a directed union, one layer beyond any single presentation currently built). `lake build` (whole project) green, zero `sorry`. #### Exercise 8.26
* **Mathematical Target:** discuss the "pay-off" for `U` ‚Äî untyped `Œª`-calculus translated into `U` via the end-of-Definition-8.9 equations, and the whole of typed `Œª`-calculus retranslated back into `U` "with the aid of projections" (hint: `f:D_a‚ÜíD_b` becomes `f=b‚àòf‚àòa`; `Œªx^{D_a}.œÉ` becomes `Œªx.b(œÉ'[a(x)/x])`, checking this "has the right type").
* **Lean File:** `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise826.lean`
* **Proof Notes:** **A genuinely expository exercise** ("discuss in more detail"), unlike 8.17‚Äì8.25's crisp existence claims ‚Äî formalized as the three checkable pieces of Scott's already-sketched scheme. **(1) The end-of-lecture equations, self-hosted in `ùí∞`**: `Uapply u x := evalMap(j_‚Üí(u), x)` (application, decode-then-apply via `jArrow`) and `Ulam f := i_‚Üí(toFilter f)` (abstraction, encode via `iArrow`); the actual content beyond notation is *faithfulness* ‚Äî `Uapply_Ulam : Uapply (Ulam f) x = f(x)`, i.e. `ùí∞`'s internal `Œª`-calculus computes the same thing as the outside one, using only `jArrow_comp_iArrow : j_‚Üí‚àòi_‚Üí=I` (Definition 8.9) and `evalMap_apply` (Theorem 3.11). **(2) The abstraction recipe and "has the right type"** (the technical heart of the hint), generalized to *any* neighbourhood system `E` and retractions `a,b:E‚ÜíE`: `translateAbs a b body := b‚àòbody‚àòa` (Scott's `Œªx.b(œÉ'[a(x)/x])`), and `translateAbs_sandwich` shows it *always* satisfies the defining sandwich equation `b‚àòf‚àòa=f` regardless of `body` ‚Äî pure associativity + idempotence (`a‚àòa=a`,`b‚àòb=b`, `Definition 8.1`'s `IsRetraction`), mirroring Scott's own one-line proof style for Proposition 8.10. The matching claim for **application**, `translateApp_hasType`: if `f=b‚àòf‚àòa` and `x` already has type `D_a` (`a(x)=x`), then `f(x)` already has type `D_b` (`b(f(x))=f(x)`) ‚Äî a one-line corollary via `toElementMap_comp` twice. A sanity check `translateAbs_idMap` covers the base case (a bare variable, `body:=id`, translates to `b‚àòa`). **(3) The correspondence `f=b‚àòf‚àòa` really is `D_a‚ÜíD_b`**: *not new content* ‚Äî cited directly from Proposition 8.10(b)'s pre-existing `arrowComb_elementIso`/`finitaryProjection_arrowComb` (`Proposition810b.lean`), which already produces exactly `(D_a‚ÜíD_b).Element‚âÉo{f‚à£(a‚Üíb)(f)=f}` for finitary projections `a,b`. **Deliberately out of scope**: a full formal syntax + typing judgment + structural induction assembling (1)‚Äì(3) into "every typed term translates correctly" ‚Äî the induction is a routine unfolding of (1)‚Äì(2) at each constructor (with `+`/`√ó` following `‚Üí`'s pattern exactly, since `translateAbs_sandwich` only needs `IsRetraction`, already established for `sumComb`/`prodComb` too in `Proposition810.lean`), not itself a new mathematical question, matching this project's convention of deferring open-ended "build a term language" scaffolding to prose (cf. Theorem 8.6/Exercise 8.23/8.25's deferred effectiveness clauses). `lake build` (whole project, 3197 jobs) green, zero `sorry`. Axiom audit: `Uapply_Ulam` `‚äÜ {propext, Classical.choice, Quot.sound}` (inherited from `U`, not new); `translateAbs_sandwich`/`translateApp_hasType`/`translateAbs_idMap` fully choice-free `‚äÜ {propext, Quot.sound}` (mention no `U`-specific object at all).

#### Exercise 8.27
* **Mathematical Target:** (Suggested by James Donahue.) Define computable *infinite* cartesian products over `U`. Regard `sub` (Theorem 8.6) as a finitary projection of `U` whose fixed points are exactly all the finitary projections; a map `d = sub‚àòd‚àòsub` is a "polymorphic type" (since `t` a finitary projection `‚üπ` `d(t)` one too). The *continuous product* of all these types is `{x ‚à£ ‚àÄt, x(t) = d(t)(x(t))}`. Define `ŒÝ = Œªd.Œªx.Œªt. sub(d(sub(t)))(x(sub(t)))`. Show that for `d` a polymorphic type, `ŒÝ(d)` is a type (hint: `ŒÝ(d)` is easily a projection; the hard part is showing it is *finitary*). This is the **last exercise in the book** (the text ends immediately after it).
* **Lean File:** `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise827.lean`
* **Proof Notes:** Fully closed, and in fact **strictly stronger than asked**: `isFinitaryProjection_piU` proves `ŒÝ(d)` is a type for *every* `d : ùí∞‚Üíùí∞`, not only polymorphic `d` ‚Äî `IsPolymorphicType`/`polymorphicType_apply_mem_fix` are formalized (Scott's own justification for the exercise's setup) but never needed by the finitary-ness proof itself. Split exactly along Scott's own hint ("it is easy to check that `ŒÝ(d)` is a projection; the problem is to show it is *finitary*") ‚Äî see sub-rows **8.27(a)** and **8.27(b)** (with its sub-plan **8.27(b)(0)‚Äì(b)(5)**), all Pass.


#### Exercise 8.27(a)
* **Mathematical Target:** "It is easy to check that `ŒÝ(d)` is a projection" (Scott's own hint) ‚Äî established *unconditionally for every* `d : ùí∞ ‚Üí ùí∞`, not only polymorphic `d`; includes the exercise's opening sentence (`sub` regarded as a finitary projection of `ùí∞` itself, fixed points = exactly the finitary projections) and the construction of `ŒÝ` as a combinator.
* **Lean File:** `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise827.lean`
* **Proof Notes:** *(1) `sub` regarded as a combinator on `ùí∞`*: `subU := i_‚Üí‚àòsubApprox‚àòj_‚Üí` (conjugating Thm 8.6(b)'s `subApprox:(ùí∞‚Üíùí∞)‚Üí(ùí∞‚Üíùí∞)` through the fixed pair `i_‚Üí,j_‚Üí` of Def 8.9, the *same* recipe Def 8.9 itself uses for `a‚Üíb`). New reusable gadget `isProjection_conjArrow`/`isRetraction_conjArrow`/`le_idMap_conjArrow` (pure `comp_assoc` algebra + `j_‚Üí‚àòi_‚Üí=I`/`i_‚Üí‚àòj_‚Üí‚â§I`) transports *any* projection of `(ùí∞‚Üíùí∞)` to one of `ùí∞`, giving `isProjection_subU` for free; reused verbatim below for `piU d`. `subUFixIso : Fix(subU)‚âÉoFix(subApprox)` (needs only `j_‚Üí‚àòi_‚Üí=I`, no inequality on `i_‚Üí‚àòj_‚Üí`) composed with Thm 8.6(b)(ii)'s own `subApproxFixIso`/`isFinitary_subApprox` gives `isFinitaryProjection_subU` and identifies `Fix(subU)` with `{f‚à£sub f=f}` = (Thm 8.6(a)) exactly the finitary projections ‚Äî Exercise 8.27's opening sentence, in full. *(2) polymorphic types*: `IsPolymorphicType d := subU.comp(d.comp subU)=d`; `polymorphicType_apply_mem_fix` formalizes the exercise's own justification ("`t` finitary projection `‚üπ` `d(t)` too") via a clean general fact, `toElementMap_mem_fix_of_isRetraction_sandwich` (any `a‚àòg‚àòa` for idempotent `a` lands in `Fix(a)`, generalizing Ex 8.26's `translateApp_hasType`). *(3) the `ŒÝ` combinator*: transcribed verbatim from Scott's formula via `curry`/`evalMap`/`paired` exactly as `Exercise825FixedPoint.lean`'s `RMap` (`piDUncurried`/`piD:=curry(piDUncurried d)`/closed-form `piDApply d f`/value lemma `toApproxMap_toElementMap_piD`), then conjugated through `i_‚Üí,j_‚Üí` (`piU d`) to land in `ùí∞` itself. *(4) "it is easy to check `ŒÝ(d)` is a projection" (Scott's hint) ‚Äî proved, and proved **unconditionally for every `d`**, not just polymorphic `d`*: the key lemma `isFinitaryProjection_decode_subU` shows `j_‚Üí(subU(z))` decodes to a genuine finitary projection for *any* `z` (from `subU`'s bare idempotency + Step 1), which alone drives both `isRetraction_piD` (idempotence chase via `piDApply_toElementMap_eq`, reducing to `P‚àòP=P` for the shared "type at `t`" `P`) and `le_idMap_piD` (monotonicity chase: `subU(t)‚äët` then `P‚â§I`). `isProjection_piU` then drops out "for free" via the Step-1 conjugation gadget. Axiom audit: `‚äÜ{propext,Classical.choice,Quot.sound}` (inherited from `ùí∞` itself, no new source).


#### Exercise 8.27(b)
* **Mathematical Target:** "The problem is to show it is *finitary*" (Scott's own hint) ‚Äî for `d` a polymorphic type, `ŒÝ(d)` (equivalently `piU d`) is finitary, i.e. `IsFinitary (piU d)`; combined with 8.27(a)'s `isProjection_piU`, this completes the exercise's statement "`ŒÝ(d)` is a type."
* **Lean File:** `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise827.lean`; umbrella ‚Äî see sub-rows **8.27(b)(0)‚Äì(b)(5)** below, all Pass
* **Proof Notes:** Closed via the strategic pivot described below, **without ever needing a fresh dependent-product `NeighborhoodSystem`** and, remarkably, **without ever needing `d`'s polymorphism**: `isFinitaryProjection_piD`/`isFinitaryProjection_piU` hold for *every* `d : ùí∞‚Üíùí∞`. Also addresses, in `Exercise827.lean`'s module docstring (no separate lemma needed), Scott's parenthetical "why does this equation mean `x` is in the product?" ‚Äî `x(t)=d(t)(x(t))` unwinds via Ex 8.26's `Uapply` to `x(t)‚ààFix(D_{d(t)})`, i.e. `x` is a genuine dependent section. **The strategic pivot that made this tractable:** rather than constructing a fresh dependent-product `NeighborhoodSystem` ex nihilo, target **Theorem 8.5**'s step-closure formula (ii) for `a := piD d` directly (`Theorem85.lean`'s `finitaryProjection_iff_formula` ‚Äî the `(ii)‚üπ(i)` direction `isFinitaryProjection_of_formula` needs *only* the formula, no external witness domain, and automatically supplies `fixedNbhd (piD d)` as the correct witness). This turned "invent new domain theory" into "compute with `piD d`'s own `.rel`," matching the shape of every other finitary-closure proof in the project. Full subgoal breakdown and the resolution of the (b)(3) obstruction are in sub-rows (b)(0)‚Äì(b)(5) below and `HANDOFF.md`'s 2026-07-07 checkpoints.


#### Exercise 8.27(b)(0)
* **Mathematical Target:** `Fix(piU d) ‚âÉo Fix(piD d)` ‚Äî reduces "`piU d` is finitary" to "`piD d` is finitary."
* **Lean File:** `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise827.lean`
* **Proof Notes:** Cheap, mechanical: `piUFixIso` copies Step 1's `subUFixIso` recipe verbatim, substituting `piD d`/`piU d` for `subApprox`/`subU` (both built by the identical `i_‚Üí‚àò(-)‚àòj_‚Üí` conjugation, so every step transfers unchanged) ‚Äî `toElementMap_piU`/`piD_fix_of_piU_fix`/`piU_fix_of_piD_fix` mirror `toElementMap_subU`/`subApprox_fix_of_subU_fix`/`subU_fix_of_subApprox_fix` line-for-line. Packaged as **`isFinitary_piU_of_isFinitary_piD`** (mirrors `isFinitary_subU`'s use of `subUFixIso`), so Exercise 8.27(b)(1) onward need only establish `IsFinitary (piD d)` for `d` polymorphic. `lake build Scott1980.Neighborhood.Exercise827` green, zero `sorry`. Axiom audit: `‚äÜ{propext,Classical.choice,Quot.sound}` (inherited from `ùí∞`, not a new source, matching 8.27(a)).


#### Exercise 8.27(b)(1)
* **Mathematical Target:** Reduce "`piD d` is finitary" to Scott's Theorem 8.5 step-closure formula (ii): `(piD d).toElementMap x = {Y ‚àà (funSpace U U).mem ‚à£ ‚àÉX, x.mem X ‚àß X‚äÜY ‚àß X(piD d)X}`, for every `x`.
* **Lean File:** `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise827.lean`
* **Proof Notes:** A direct specialization of `Theorem85.lean`'s general `isFinitaryProjection_of_formula` (`E := funSpace U U`, `a := piD d`) ‚Äî no new proof needed beyond the specialization itself. **`isFinitaryProjection_piD_of_formula`**: formula (ii) for `piD d` ‚üπ `IsFinitaryProjection (piD d)` (the witness domain `fixedNbhd (piD d)` is produced automatically, no external construction). **`isFinitary_piU_of_formula`**: assembled with 8.27(b)(0)'s `isFinitary_piU_of_isFinitary_piD`, formula (ii) for `piD d` alone now gives `IsFinitary (piU d)` ‚Äî combined with the already-Pass 8.27(a), the *entire* exercise for `d` polymorphic. This pins down exactly what 8.27(b)(2)‚Äì(b)(3) need to supply: the `hii` hypothesis. `lake build Scott1980.Neighborhood.Exercise827` green, zero `sorry`. Axiom audit: `‚äÜ{propext,Classical.choice,Quot.sound}` (inherited from `ùí∞`, not new).


#### Exercise 8.27(b)(2)
* **Mathematical Target:** Unwind `piD d = curry (piDUncurried d)`'s neighbourhood-level relation `X (piD d) Y` between `funSpace U U`-nbhds, down to a formula in terms of `subU`'s and `d`'s own relations plus `evalMap`'s abstract defining relation.
* **Lean File:** `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise827.lean`
* **Proof Notes:** *(2a)* `curry_rel` (`FunctionSpace.lean`, pre-existing ‚Äî the abstract layer, not the Ex 7.16 coded one) already reduces `(piD d).rel X W` to a literal set-membership test `gSection (piDUncurried d) hX ‚àà W`; **`piD_rel_iff`** is the free direct specialization, no new proof. *(2b)* **`gSection_piDUncurried_rel_iff`** unwinds `gSection`'s own relation the rest of the way: `gSection_rel` reduces it to `(piDUncurried d).rel (prodNbhd X Y) Z`; the general bridge `rel_iff_mem_principal` (`Approximable.lean`) plus the general `pair_principal_eq_principal_prodNbhd` (`Exercise821.lean`, reused via a fresh, non-cyclic import ‚Äî pairing two principal elements is the principal element of the product nbhd) convert this to the *element*-level pair `pair (principal hX) (principal hY)`; `toElementMap_piDUncurried`/`toElementMap_piDApply` (both pre-existing, built from `subU`'s and `d`'s `toElementMap` actions plus `evalMap_apply`) then read off the closed form `((piDApply d (toApproxMap (principal hX))).toElementMap (principal hY)).mem Z` ‚Äî exactly "a formula in terms of `subU`'s and `d`'s own relations plus `evalMap`'s abstract defining relation," routed through the already-proven closed form rather than re-derived from scratch. **`piD_rel_self_iff`** packages (2a)+(2b) at the self-relation shape (`X (piD d) X`) that Theorem 8.5's formula (ii) actually tests ‚Äî the form 8.27(b)(3) will consume. `lake build Scott1980.Neighborhood.Exercise827` green, zero `sorry`. Axiom audit: `‚äÜ{propext,Classical.choice,Quot.sound}` (inherited from `toElementMap_piDUncurried`/`ùí∞`, not a new source).


#### Exercise 8.27(b)(3)
* **Mathematical Target:** Prove Scott's formula (ii) for `piD d` (per (b)(1)), using (b)(2)'s `.rel` formula.
* **Lean File:** `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise827.lean`; umbrella ‚Äî see sub-rows **8.27(b)(3)(a)‚Äì(b)(3)(b)** below, both Pass
* **Proof Notes:** Split into (a) the reduction + the unconditional `‚ü∏` half and (b) the `‚üπ` half; **`hii_piD`** assembles both into the full iff. Closed for *every* `d`, `d`'s polymorphism not needed. See sub-rows.


#### Exercise 8.27(b)(3)(a)
* **Mathematical Target:** Reduce `hii`'s LHS to a literal membership test, and close the `‚ü∏` half of formula (ii) for `piD d` unconditionally (for any `d`, not just polymorphic).
* **Lean File:** `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise827.lean`, `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Theorem85.lean` (one new general lemma)
* **Proof Notes:** **`piD_toElementMap_mem_iff`** reduces `hii`'s LHS to a literal membership test `piDApply d (toApproxMap x) ‚àà Y`, no abstract element-reasoning left, via `Sub8_6.toFilter_toApproxMap`/`mem_toFilter` + the already-proven `toApproxMap_toElementMap_piD`. **`mem_of_exists_rel_self`** (`Theorem85.lean`, new, genuinely general): isolated out of `isFinitaryProjection_of_formula`'s own proof ‚Äî its `‚ü∏`-branch never actually used the finitary-projection hypothesis, only `rel_iff_mem_principal`/`principal_le_of_mem`/`toElementMap_mono`/`up_mem`; now a standalone fact for *any* `a : E ‚Üí E`, no hypothesis at all (`x.mem X ‚Üí X‚äÜY ‚Üí a.rel X X ‚Üí (a.toElementMap x).mem Y`), and reused to simplify `isFinitaryProjection_of_formula`'s own proof (DRY). **`hii_easy_direction`** specializes it to `a := piD d`: the entire `‚ü∏` half of `hii` closes unconditionally, for any `d`. `lake build` green, zero `sorry`. Axiom audit: `mem_of_exists_rel_self` is **choice-free** (`‚äÜ{propext,Quot.sound}`); the `ùí∞`-specific corollaries `‚äÜ{propext,Classical.choice,Quot.sound}` as usual.


#### Exercise 8.27(b)(3)(b)
* **Mathematical Target:** Close the `‚üπ` half of formula (ii) for `piD d`: given `piDApply d (toApproxMap x) ‚àà Y`, construct `X` with `x.mem X`, `X‚äÜY`, `(piD d).rel X X`.
* **Lean File:** `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise827.lean`
* **Proof Notes:** **This is the actual mathematical content of "the problem" ‚Äî closed, for every `d`.** The obstruction diagnosed in the prior checkpoint (chasing a *single* domain witness `T_i‚äáY_i` forces the wrong, strictly weaker type-projection when testing `X`'s self-relation) is resolved by a compactness-descent argument mirroring `Theorem85.lean`'s own `(i)‚üπ(ii)` hard direction: `t := subU(‚ÜëY‚ÇÄ)` is *itself* the directed sup of its own `subU`-self-consistent approximants `scPrincipal : scFamily t ‚Üí U.Element` (`eq_iSupDirected_scPrincipal`, cofinal by `exists_rel_self_subset_of_mem` ‚Äî formula (ii) for `subU`, Ex 8.27(a)), on which `principal T = subU(‚ÜëT)` *exactly* (`subU_principal_eq_of_rel_self`, antisymmetry: `‚â§` from `subU`'s projection property, `‚â•` from self-consistency). Since `d`/`subU`/`jArrow` (bundled as `piDTypeMap`) are continuous, both the continuity witness for `x` *and* the self-relation witness for the "type at `t`" `piDType d t` (a finitary projection unconditionally, Step 4) are, by directed-sup compactness (`toElementMap_iSupDirected`+`mem_iSupDirected`, `Sub8_6.toApproxMap_rel_iSupDirected`), already witnessed at *some* single self-consistent approximant; one common refinement (`scFamily_directed`) then finds a *single* `T` where both hold simultaneously and (by self-consistency) matches exactly the type-projection `X`'s own self-test needs ‚Äî no mismatch (`exists_X_of_mem_step`, the single-pair case). `exists_X_of_mem_stepFun` assembles a general `stepFun` list by induction, combining per-pair witnesses via `x.inter_mem`/`(piD d).mono`+`.inter_right` (self-relation of an intersection of two self-related nbhds ‚Äî free, no extra consistency witness needed since `x`'s own filter already supplies one). `hii_hard_direction` destructures a general `Y` via `funSpace_mem_iff` and applies this. **`d`'s polymorphism is never used** ‚Äî the argument only needs `subU`'s own finitary-projection-ness (Ex 8.27(a)) and Step 4's unconditional `isFinitaryProjection_decode_subU`; the result is strictly stronger than what the exercise asks for. `lake build Scott1980.Neighborhood.Exercise827` green, zero `sorry`. Axiom audit: `‚äÜ{propext,Classical.choice,Quot.sound}` (inherited from `ùí∞`, not new ‚Äî checked directly on `exists_X_of_mem_step`/`hii_hard_direction`).


#### Exercise 8.27(b)(4)
* **Mathematical Target:** Assemble (b)(0)‚Äì(b)(3) into `IsFinitaryProjection (piU d)` for `d` polymorphic ‚Äî the full statement of Exercise 8.27.
* **Lean File:** `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise827.lean`
* **Proof Notes:** **`hii_piD`** combines (b)(3)(a)/(b)'s two halves into the full formula-(ii) iff for `piD d`; **`isFinitaryProjection_piD`** applies (b)(1)'s `isFinitaryProjection_piD_of_formula`; **`isFinitaryProjection_piU`** combines with (b)(0)'s `isFinitary_piU_of_isFinitary_piD` and (a)'s `isProjection_piU` ‚Äî Exercise 8.27, in full, for *every* `d` (polymorphism not required). `lake build` green, zero `sorry`.


#### Exercise 8.27(b)(5)
* **Mathematical Target:** Bookkeeping: build, axiom-audit, and close out the `arxiv.md`/`HANDOFF.md` status for 8.27(b).
* **Lean File:** `Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise827.lean`
* **Proof Notes:** `lake build` (whole project) green, zero `sorry`. `#print axioms` on `exists_X_of_mem_step`, `hii_hard_direction`, `hii_piD`, `isFinitaryProjection_piD`, `isFinitaryProjection_piU`: all `‚äÜ{propext,Classical.choice,Quot.sound}`, matching the rest of `ùí∞`-based material (not a new choice source). `Exercise827` already wired into `Domain.lean`/`Scott1980.lean`'s import graph. 8.27(b) and the umbrella 8.27 both flipped to `Pass`; dated `HANDOFF.md` checkpoint recording the resolution. The dependent-product-`NeighborhoodSystem` fallback was **not needed** ‚Äî the formula-(ii) route closed cleanly.

## Build

```bash
lake exe cache get
lake build Scott1980
python3 scripts/generate_lecture_mermaid.py --write   # sync ### Lecture ‚Ä¶ mermaid blocks in arxiv.md
bash scripts/generate_arxiv_with_code.sh   # -> arxiv_with_code.md (gitignored)
bash scripts/build_arxiv_tex.sh            # -> arxiv.tex + lean-listings/ + figures/ (gitignored)
bash scripts/build_arxiv_pdf.sh            # -> arxiv.pdf (LuaLaTeX; tracked) + dist/arxiv_submit.zip
bash scripts/package_arxiv_submit.sh       # -> dist/arxiv_submit.zip only (skips PDF)
```

* [Exercise722.lean](https://github.com/catskillsresearch/scott1980/blob/main/Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise722.lean) ‚Äî algebraic core (`Ssys`, `mulElem`, `emb`; infinite-word discussion)
* [Exercise722Regular.lean](https://github.com/catskillsresearch/scott1980/blob/main/Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise722Regular.lean) ‚Äî `SExpr` syntax, `denote`, `matchesB`, regular-event characterization
* [Exercise722DFA.lean](https://github.com/catskillsresearch/scott1980/blob/main/Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise722DFA.lean) ‚Äî leaf DFAs (`sigmaDFA`, `singleDFA`, inter/compl)
* [Exercise722Cat.lean](https://github.com/catskillsresearch/scott1980/blob/main/Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise722Cat.lean) ‚Äî concatenation ŒµNFA (`catEps`)
* [Exercise722Decide.lean](https://github.com/catskillsresearch/scott1980/blob/main/Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise722Decide.lean) ‚Äî uniform `toNFA`, emptiness/consistency Bool deciders
* [Exercise722Words.lean](https://github.com/catskillsresearch/scott1980/blob/main/Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise722Words.lean) ‚Äî bounded word enumeration for search
* [Exercise722Equiv.lean](https://github.com/catskillsresearch/scott1980/blob/main/Scott1980/Neighborhood/Exercise722Equiv.lean) ‚Äî choice-free `Finset`-subset-construction simulation of `toNFA e`; `subsetB`/`interEqB` language-equivalence deciders (**7.22k**)

### Lecture VIII support modules (recursion-theory / presentation helpers)

* [DAtomDecidable.lean](https://github.com/catskillsresearch/scott1980/blob/main/Scott1980/Neighborhood/DAtomDecidable.lean) ‚Äî Theorem 8.8(b) Part 5 ‚Äî decidable `D`-side atom emptiness
* [IntervalPrimrec.lean](https://github.com/catskillsresearch/scott1980/blob/main/Scott1980/Neighborhood/IntervalPrimrec.lean) ‚Äî Theorem 8.8(b) ‚Äî primitive-recursive interval-code arithmetic for `ùí∞`
* [LevelSetPrimrec.lean](https://github.com/catskillsresearch/scott1980/blob/main/Scott1980/Neighborhood/LevelSetPrimrec.lean) ‚Äî Exercise 8.12(b) ‚Äî `V`'s computable presentation
* [MinLevel.lean](https://github.com/catskillsresearch/scott1980/blob/main/Scott1980/Neighborhood/MinLevel.lean) ‚Äî Exercise 8.12(e)(d)(i) ‚Äî minimal-level canonicalization
* [RationalPrimrec.lean](https://github.com/catskillsresearch/scott1980/blob/main/Scott1980/Neighborhood/RationalPrimrec.lean) ‚Äî a choice-free G√∂del numbering of `‚Ñö`, primitive-recursive comparison/max/min
* [RecursiveCross.lean](https://github.com/catskillsresearch/scott1980/blob/main/Scott1980/Neighborhood/RecursiveCross.lean) ‚Äî a choice-free primitive-recursive "cross-combine" of two coded lists
* [SplitU.lean](https://github.com/catskillsresearch/scott1980/blob/main/Scott1980/Neighborhood/SplitU.lean) ‚Äî Theorem 8.8(b) Part 4 ‚Äî an explicit, deterministic `splitU`
* [SplitV.lean](https://github.com/catskillsresearch/scott1980/blob/main/Scott1980/Neighborhood/SplitV.lean) ‚Äî Exercise 8.12(e)(b)/(e)(d)(ii) ‚Äî a computable canonical bisection of `V`
* [UBisection2.lean](https://github.com/catskillsresearch/scott1980/blob/main/Scott1980/Neighborhood/UBisection2.lean) ‚Äî Exercise 8.12(f) prerequisite ‚Äî a presentation-independent canonical bisection of `ùí∞`
* [UComputablePresentation.lean](https://github.com/catskillsresearch/scott1980/blob/main/Scott1980/Neighborhood/UComputablePresentation.lean) ‚Äî Theorem 8.8(b) Part 3 ‚Äî `ùí∞` (Definition 8.7) has a genuine `ComputablePresentation`
* [VDiff.lean](https://github.com/catskillsresearch/scott1980/blob/main/Scott1980/Neighborhood/VDiff.lean) ‚Äî Exercise 8.12(c)/(d) support ‚Äî a computable `V`-side set-difference
